=== LOA and SOP Quick Reference ===
--General--
.loa .note ZFW_IDS |\n| D10-ZFW Restrictions: [gate][dfw/dal/esat/wsat] |\n| OKC Restrictions: okczfw or zfwokc or okczkc |\n| All others: zfw[fac] i.e. zfwabi |\n| ZHU LOA: zfwxxxyyy where xxx is the arrival airport/area and yyy is the sending ZFW area
.loaref .OPENURL https://zfwartcc.net/file/14-loa-reference-table.pdf
.zfwiah .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Must enter sending area [JEN, DAL, CQY] ex zfwiahdal |\n
.zfwhou .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Must enter sending area [JEN, DAL, CQY, GGG] ex zfwhoujen |\n
.zfwsat .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Must enter sending area [JEN, DAL, CQY] ex zfwsatcqy |\n
.zfwaus .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Must enter sending area [JEN, DAL, CQY] ex zfwausdal |\n
.okcscratch .OPENURL https://zfwartcc.net/file/44.pdf



--D10-ZFW LOA--
.bypdfw .note ZFW_IDS BONHAM GATE DFW ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA SEEVR(S)/BRDJE(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) WILBR STAR...CROSS BRDJE @ 110 (S)/FUNKY @ 110 (N)\n (Prop) WILBR STAR...CROSS BRDJE @ 080
.bypdal .note ZFW_IDS BONHAM GATE DAL ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA HIBIL(S)/CRIKT(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) FINGR STAR...CROSS FINGR @ 090 \n (Prop) FINGR STAR...CROSS FINGR @ 060
.bypesat .note ZFW_IDS BONHAM GATE EAST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) SLANT STAR...CROSS FINGR @ 080\n (Jet Non-RNAV) FINGR STAR...CROSS FINGR @ 080 \n (Prop) FINGR/SLANT STAR...CROSS FINGR @ 060
.bypwsat .note ZFW_IDS  BONHAM GATE WEST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) TRUUK STAR...CROSS SASIE @ 110 (S)/ @ 100 (N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) SASIE STAR...CROSS FINGR @ 110 (S)/ @ 100 (N) \n (Prop) SASIE/TRUUK STAR...CROSS SASIE @ 060

.cqydfw .note ZFW_IDS CEDAR CREEK GATE DFW ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA BEREE(S)/WHINY(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) CQY STAR...CROSS WARDZ @ 110 (S)/HOWDY @ 110 (N)\n (Prop) (S) YEAGR STAR...CROSS YEAGR @ 070/(N) CQY STAR...CROSS HOWDY @ 070
.cqydal .note ZFW_IDS  CEDAR CREEK GATE DAL ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA REDDN(S)/MNNDO(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) YEAGR STAR...CROSS YEAGR @ 080 \n (Prop RNAV) REDDN(S)/MNNDO(N) STAR...CROSS ORVLL @ 060 \n (Prop) YEAGR STAR...CROSS YEAGR @ 060
.cqyesat .note ZFW_IDS CEDAR CREEK GATE EAST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) LOADS(S)/EESAT(N) STAR...CROSS YEAGR @ 080\n (Jet Non-RNAV) YEAGR STAR...CROSS YEAGR @ 080 \n (Prop) LOADS(S)/EESAT(N) STAR...CROSS YEAGR @ 060
.cqywsat .note ZFW_IDS CEDAR CREEK GATE WEST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) REEKO STAR...CROSS DODJE @ 090 (S)/ @ 120 (N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) DODJE STAR...CROSS DODJE @ 090 (S)/ @ 120 (N) \n (Prop) REEKO/DODJE STAR...CROSS DODJE @ 060

.jendfw .note ZFW_IDS GLEN ROSE GATE DFW ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA BOOVE(S)/SOCKK(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) On TTT219R...CROSS TTT219/42 @ 170 (S)/ @ 090 (N)\n (Prop RNAV) ZROBA STAR...CROSS BOOVE @ 060 \n (Prop) On TTT219R...CROSS TTT219/42 @ 060
.jendal .note ZFW_IDS GLEN ROSE GATE DAL ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA BACHR(S)/DRYYE(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) On CVE213R...CROSS CVE213/47 @ 100 (S)/ @ 120 (N) \n (Prop RNAV) SWVAY STAR...CROSS KNEAD @ 070 \n (Prop) On CVE213R...CROSS CVE213/47 @ 070
.jenesat .note ZFW_IDS GLEN ROSE GATE EAST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) SWVAY STAR...CROSS KNEAD @ 100 (S)/ @ 120 (N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) On CVE213R...CROSS CVE213/47 @ 100 (S)/ @ 120 (N) \n (Prop RNAV) SWVAY STAR...CROSS KNEAD @ 070 \n (Prop) On CVE213R...CROSS CVE213/47 @ 070
.jenwsat .note ZFW_IDS GLEN ROSE GATE WEST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) LIKES STAR...CROSS SLUGG @ 080 (S)/ @ 060 (N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) On FUZ222R...CROSS FUZ222/38 @ 080 (S)/ @ 060 (N) \n (Prop RNAV) LIKES STAR...CROSS SLUGG @ 050 \n (Prop) On FUZ222R...CROSS FUZ222/38 @ 050

.ukwdfw .note ZFW_IDS BOWIE GATE DFW ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA VKTRY(S)/JOVEM(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) UKW STAR...CROSS BEWTS @ 100 (S)/HIKAY @ 110 (N)\n (Prop) UKW STAR...CROSS VKTRY @ 060
.ukwdal .note ZFW_IDS BOWIE GATE DAL ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) DESCEND VIA JFRYE(S)/HERBZ(N)\n (Jet Non-RNAV) GREGS STAR...CROSS GREGS @ 110(S)/ @ 100 (N) \n (Prop) GREGS/JFRYE STAR...CROSS GREGS @ 070
.ukwesat .note ZFW_IDS BOWIE GATE EAST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) JFRYE STAR...CROSS GREGS @ 100\n (Jet Non-RNAV) GREGS STAR...CROSS GREGS @ 110(S)/ @ 100 (N) \n (Prop) GREGS/JFRYE STAR...CROSS GREGS @ 070
.ukwwsat .note ZFW_IDS BOWIE GATE WEST SATELLITE ARRIVALS \n (Jet RNAV) WESAT STAR...CROSS MOTZA @ 080\n (Jet Non-RNAV) MOTZA STAR...CROSS MOTZA @ 080 \n (Prop) WESAT/MOTZA STAR...CROSS MOTZA @ 060

.zfwd10 .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Direction of flow is determined by direction of landing at DFW |\n| Overflights must be routed around TRACON airspace |\n| MID SHIFT: ZFW may clear aircraft direct to destination airport descending to 110 (Jets) or any altitude below 100 (Props) |\n
.d10zfw .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Jet departures may be stacked up to two per stack provided that the aircraft with the most completed flying miles is on top and ZFW is informed of the stack prior to communication change |\n| E/W departures may be cleared to the first fix outside of the TRACON boundary |\n| N/S departures must be on route except for ADM, ACT, WINDU, ELLVR, BRDEN |\n| Prop departures may be on headings through gate, ZFW has control for turns |\n| MID SHIFT: N/S/E departures may be cleared to destinations inside CONUS. |\n


--OKC-ZFW LOA--
.zfwokc .note ZFW_IDS \n| RNAV - DESCENDING VIA RNAV ARRIVAL |\n| Conv - On appropriate IRW radial @ 100 OR 060 if below 090 |\n
.okczfw .note ZFW_IDS \n| RNAV - On RNAV Departure |\n| Conv - Cleared to first valid fix |\n| All aircraft climbing to 150 or req altitude |\n

===Phraseology Helpers===
.refuel .note ZFW_IDS |\n| "Cleared to conduct refueling along [track] maintain block FL XXX through FL YYY" |\n| Provide radar assistance and vertical separation between flights until TANKER declares MARSA with RECEIVER. Ensure RECEIVER squawks standby. RECEIVER should move to lowest altitude in block before requesting to resume their flight. |\n|
.marsa .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Military Assumes Resonsibility for Separation of Aircraft |\n| Ensure IFR separation is provided until MARSA is declared by flight |\n| Continue to separate MARSA flight from non-participating aircraft |\n|
.overhead .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Overhead/Carrier Break |\n| "Report initial" (May specify distance but usually 3-5nm from runway) IFR is automatically cancelled at the initial |\n||\n| "Break at [specified point], report the break" |\n|
.moa .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Example: "Cleared Lancer MOA, maintain block 7000 through FL190." |\n| Aircraft should contact prior to airspace exit |\n|
.mtr .note ZFW_IDS |\n| Example: "Cleared into IR-117, maintain IR-117 altitudes." |\n| When aircraft is ready to leave IR: Issue IFR clearance to destination. |\n|

---Pre-Clearance---
.clr Clearance on request number $1
.clravail Clearance available, advise when ready to copy. 
.amend I have a amendment to your flight plan, advise ready to copy.
.fullam I have a full re-route clearence for your flight plan, advise ready to copy.

---IFR clearence---
(Departure Sector ID)
.ifrcv Cleared to the $arr via $route, climb via SID, Departure $freq($1), $squawk

.ifrma Cleared to the $arr via $route, maintain $1, then expect $cruise 10 mins after departure, departure $freq($2), squawk $squawk

.ifrex Cleared to the $arr via $route, climb via SID except maintain $1, Departure $freq($2), squawk $squawk

.ifrcvdo Cleared to the $arr via $route, climb via SID, Departure 122.8, $squawk

.ifrmado Cleared to the $arr via $route, maintain $1, then expect $cruise 10 mins after departure, departure 122.8, squawk $squawk

.ifrexdo Cleared to the $arr via $route, climb via SID except maintain $1, Departure 122.8, squawk $squawk

.rcor Readback correct, push and start at pilot's discression, contact Ground on $freq ($1) for taxi. 

.rcorg Readback correct, push and start at pilot's discression, call ready for taxi, expect runway $1 for departure. 

.h4rel Readback correct, hold for release. Advise this frequency when number 1 for the runway. Frequency change approved.
-----Departure Release - .rel4dep Released at (# of minutes from current time) Void at (# of minutes from current time). Standard entry = .rel4dep 0 10
.rel4dep Released for departure at $ftime($1), clearance void if not off by $ftime($2), time now $time. Frequency change approved.

.vfrbent Cleared to enter the Dallas-Fort Worth Bravo airspace, squawk $squawk
.vfrbdep Cleared out of the Dallas-Fort Worth Bravo airspace, maintain VFR at or below $1, departure frequency $freq($2), squawk $squawk

---Ground---

.td Runway $1, taxi via $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.ta Taxi via $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9 to the ramp
.tapd Taxi to the ramp at pilot s discretion, cross all runways
.hs Hold short $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.hp Hold position
.ct Continue taxi
.gwt Give way to $1
.crs Cross runway $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9

---Local Control---

.ctl Runway $1, cleared to land. Wind $winds
.cto Runway $1, cleared for takeoff. Wind $winds
.ctorh Fly runway heading, runway $1, cleared for takeoff. Wind $winds
.ctohdg Fly heading $2, runway $1, cleared for takeoff. Wind $winds
.ctor RNAV to $2, runway $1, cleared for takeoff. Wind $winds
.ctomrt Make right traffic, runway $1, cleared for takeoff. Wind $winds
.ctomlt Make left traffic, runway $1, cleared for takeoff. Wind $winds
.ctoc Cancel takeoff clearance
.gafpm Go around, fly the published missed approach
.gavec Go around. Fly heading $1, maintain $2, contact $radioname($3) $freq($3)
.luaw Runway $1, line up and wait 
.wel Turn $1 when able
.xrhs Cross runway $1, hold short $2, contact $radioname($3) $freq($3) on the other side
.xr Cross runway $1, contact $radioname($2) $freq($2) on the other side
.elb Enter left base runway $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.erb Enter right base runway $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.erd Enter right downwind runway $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.eld Enter left downwind runway $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9

---Radar (TRACON) ---
.rc Radar contact
.rcsalt  Radar contact, say altitude leaving. 
.rcv Radar contact $dist($1)nm $bearing($1) of $1 altitude $calt
.rcl Radar contact lost
.cils $distance($1)nm from $1, fly heading $2 maintain $3 until established, cleared ILS runway $4 approach. $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.rnvptac Cleared direct $1, cross $1 at or above $2, cleared $3 runway $4 approach.
.apat $arr airport is at $oclock($arr), $dist($arr)nm, report in sight
.cvis Cleared visual approach runway $1
.notwrifr No visible traffic between you and the field, report IFR cancellation in the air or on the ground this frequency. Frequency change approved.
.dept Depart $1 heading $2
.vr Vectors for $1 $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.xapp Expect $1 runway $2, $arr altimeter $altim($arr)
.xils Expect ILS runway $1
.xvis Expect visual approach runway $1
.tra Taffic alert, $1 o'clock $2 miles, advise you $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9 immediately
.laa Low altitude alert. Check your altitude immediately. The MVA in your area is $1
.veratis Verify you have information $1
.tr Turn right heading $1
.tl Turn left heading $1 
.prd Proceed direct $1 
.cd Cleared direct $1
.fh Fly heading $1
.fhjr Fly heading $1, join the $2 $3 radial $4
.cm Climb and maintain $1
.cma Climb and maintain $1,000
.dm Descend and maintain $1
.dma Descend and maintain $1,000
.dmpd Descend at pilot's discretion, maintain $1
.vfrcan Radar service terminated, squawk and maintain VFR, frequency change approved.
.tll Turn left heading $1, intercept Runway $2 localizer
.trl Turn right heading $1, intercept Runway $2 localizer
.fhl Fly heading $1, intercept Runway $2 localizer

---Center---
.x Cross $1 at and maintain $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.xaoa Cross $1 at or above $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9
.xspd Cross $1 at and maintain $2 at $3 KTS
.xdme Cross $1 DME of $2 at $3 
.dvia Descend via the $1 arrival
.dviax Descend via the $1 arrival except $2
.cmf Climb and maintain FL$1
.dmf Descend and maintain FL$1

---Holding---

.holdap Cleared to $1, hold $2 of $1 as published. Expect further clearance at $3 zulu

---MSC---
.ho Contact $radioname($1) on $freq($1), have a good flight! 
.hodep Contact Departure  $freq($1) Cya!
.depoff No departure control avilable, monitor unicom 122.8, Thanks for flying Fort Worth! 
.rts Reset transponder, $squawk

.ecc You're exiting Class C airspace, radar service is terminated, squawk VFR, frequency change approved, thanks for flying Fort Worth!
.close **NOTAM** $radioname ($1) will be closing in $2 minutes

.closing **NOTAM** $radioname ($1) is closing at $2
.shift **NOTAM** $radioname ($1) shift change in progress
.rst Radar service is terminated, squawk VFR, frequency change approved

.sas Say indicated air speed
.sms Say mach
.spo Say position
.smc Sqwawk mode C
.ss Squawk standby

.sqi Squawk $squawk and Ident
.sq Squawk $squawk

.rpt Report over $1
.rptabm Report abeam $1
.ifrcangnd IFR cancellation received, thanks for flying.
.icanair IFR cancellation received. Radar service terminated, squawk and maintain VFR, frequency change approved, good day.

.bear You are $bear($1) from $1
.clock $1 is at your $oclock($1)
.route $route

.ratis  Report receiving ATIS $1
.rmatis Report receiving ATIS $atiscode
.cyrv Can you recieve voice?

---HELP COMMANDS---

.helphub .MSG |\n|==========HELP HUB==========|\n|[D10 AIRSPACE MAPS].d10help|\n| |\n|[CTR COMMANDS].ctrhelp|\n| |\n| |\n| to look up a airline .id |\n| 
.d10help .MSG |\n|==========D10 HELP==========|\n|[[SPECIFIC AIRSPACE MAPS]].(AR/DR/SAT/FED)(N/S) ex. "ARs" or "SATn"|\n| |\n|[[SPECIFIC ARRIVAL MAPS]].(Name of Arrival) ex. ".JOVEM4" (Only for DFW DAL & OKC)|\n| |\n|[[COMBINED RNAV ARRIVALS]].dfwarr(n/s) .dalarr(n/s) ex. ".dfwarrn"|\n|(DFW Conventional Arrivals).dfwarrcon , (DAL Conventional Arrivals).dalarrcon|\n| |\n|[D10 North/South Flow Map Toggle] (.d10n) or (.d10s)
.ctrhelp .MSG |\n|==========CTR HELP==========|\n|[ZFW HI SPLITS].zfwhi|\n|[ZFW LO SPLITS].zfwlo|\n| |\n|[ZHU SPLIT].zhusplit|\n|[ZME SPLIT].zmesplit or (HI).zmehi or (LO).zmelo|\n|[ZAB SPLIT].zabsplit|\n| |\n|[MIA MAP].mia|\n|[ALL MVAs].mva|\n|[ALL TRACON BOUNDARIES].appbound|\n|[ALL AIRSPACE].airspace|\n| |\n|[TRACON RVMs].rvm|\n|[D10 RVMs](.d10n) or (.d10s)|\n|[OKC RVMs](.okcn) or (.okcs)|\n| |\n|[VOR NAMES].(VOR ID)n ex. "TTTn" or "IRWn"

.d .msg $atccallsign($1) *** $dep $aircraft $2 $3 $4 $5 $6 $7 $8 $9 $route $alt
------------------------------------- aircraft equipment sufx --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
.slanta .echo DME, transponder with mode C, no RVSM
.slantg .echo GNSS, transponder with mode C, no RVSM
.slanti .echo RNAV, no GNSS, transponder with mode C, no RVSM
.slantl .echo GNSS, transponder with mode C, RVSM
.slantp .echo TACAN, transponder with mode C, no RVSM
.slantu .echo no DME, transponder with mode C, no RVSM
.slantw .echo no GNSS or RNAV, transponder with mode C, RVSM
.slantz .echo RNAV, no GNSS, transponder with mode C, RVSM
